#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x0001 [0x03] Work_Zone[1] = 0*
  1: 0x0006 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[6] = 0*
  2: 0x000B [0x24] CREATE_DIALOG(message_id=7199*, default_option=0*, option_flags=0*)
     "Choose a menu. [View fellow parameters./Set fellow event parameters./Set fellow battle parameters./Set fellow equipment./Set fellow bond value./View fellow graphics./Reset fellow battle parameters.]"
  3: 0x0012 [0x25] WAIT_DIALOG_SELECT()
  4: 0x0013 [0x02] IF !(Work_Zone[0] == 0*) GOTO 0x0052
  5: 0x001B [0x1A] CALL_SUBROUTINE(address=0x1E57)
```
